<script type="7abd233a2e8179b516de0d2b-text/javascript">
(function() {
    const title = document.querySelector(".title-color-cstm");
    if (!title) return;

    const text = title.textContent.trim();
    const lastSpaceIndex = text.lastIndexOf(" ");

    if (lastSpaceIndex !== -1) {
        const firstPart = text.substring(0, lastSpaceIndex);
        const lastWord = text.substring(lastSpaceIndex + 1);

        title.innerHTML = firstPart + ' <span class="last-word">' + lastWord + '</span>';
    }
})();
</script>

					<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default"><a href="https://upgrading.org/software-and-operating-systems/best-enterprise-management-software-worth-using/">17 Best Enterprise Management Software Worth Using</a></h2>				</div>

					<p>Enterprise management software is now a common part of how large businesses plan, track, and deliver work. Many companies are moving away from manual methods like spreadsheets, emails, and frequent status meetings because these approaches slow work and create confusion				</div>

					<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default"><a href="https://upgrading.org/software-and-operating-systems/types-of-operating-systems-with-examples/">9 Types of Operating Systems With Examples</a></h2>				</div>

					<p>Every digital device relies on a core system that keeps everything running smoothly in the background. Without it, computers, smartphones, tablets, and servers would be unable to manage software, hardware resources, memory allocation, or user interactions effectively. Many people use				</div>

				const lazyloadRunObserver = () => {
					const lazyloadBackgrounds = document.querySelectorAll( `.e-con.e-parent:not(.e-lazyloaded)` );
					const lazyloadBackgroundObserver = new IntersectionObserver( ( entries ) => {
						entries.forEach( ( entry ) => {
							if ( entry.isIntersecting ) {
								let lazyloadBackground = entry.target;
								if( lazyloadBackground ) {
									lazyloadBackground.classList.add( 'e-lazyloaded' );
								}
								lazyloadBackgroundObserver.unobserve( entry.target );
							}
						});
					}, { rootMargin: '200px 0px 200px 0px' } );
					lazyloadBackgrounds.forEach( ( lazyloadBackground ) => {
						lazyloadBackgroundObserver.observe( lazyloadBackground );
					} );
				};
				const events = [
					'DOMContentLoaded',
					'elementor/lazyload/observe',
				];
				events.forEach( ( event ) => {
					document.addEventListener( event, lazyloadRunObserver );
				} );

  document.querySelectorAll('.e-loop-nothing-found-message').forEach(nothingEl => {

      const section = nothingEl.closest('.elementor-section, .elementor-top-section, .category-sec-1, .category-sec-2');

    }
  });
});

<script type="7abd233a2e8179b516de0d2b-text/javascript">
jQuery(document).on('elementor/popup/show', function (event, popupId) {

    if (popupId !== 3265) return; // your popup ID

    const popupSelector = '#elementor-popup-modal-' + popupId;

    let attempts = 0;
    const maxAttempts = 20;

    const focusTimer = setInterval(function () {
        const $input = jQuery(popupSelector).find('input.e-search-input');

        if ($input.length) {
            // force focus
            $input[0].focus({ preventScroll: true });

            // force caret position
            const val = $input.val();
            $input.val('').val(val);

            attempts++;
        }

        if (attempts >= maxAttempts) {
            clearInterval(focusTimer);
        }
    }, 100);
});
</script>

<script type="7abd233a2e8179b516de0d2b-text/javascript">
jQuery(function($){
  var swiperEl = $('.centerd-carousel .swiper')[0];
  if(!swiperEl) return;
  function init(){
    var swiper = swiperEl.swiper;
    if(!swiper) return setTimeout(init,200);      
    swiper.params.centeredSlides = true;       
    swiper.params.slideToClickedSlide = true; 
    swiper.update();                            
  }
  init()
;
});
</script>
<script type="7abd233a2e8179b516de0d2b-text/javascript">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
  const waitForSwiper = setInterval(() => {
    const loopWrapper = document.querySelector(".p-loop-cstm");

    if (!loopWrapper) return;

    const swiperEl = loopWrapper.querySelector(".swiper");
    if (!swiperEl || !swiperEl.swiper) return;

    const swiper = swiperEl.swiper;

    const progressFill = document.querySelector(".loop-progress-fill");
    const currentSlideEl = document.querySelector(".current-slide");
    const totalSlidesEl = document.querySelector(".total-slides");

    if (!progressFill || !currentSlideEl || !totalSlidesEl) return;

    const realSlides = swiper.slides.filter(slide => 
      !slide.classList.contains("swiper-slide-duplicate")
    );

    const totalSlides = realSlides.length;
    totalSlidesEl.textContent = totalSlides;

    function updateProgress() {
      const currentIndex = swiper.realIndex + 1;
      const progress = (currentIndex / totalSlides) * 100;

      progressFill.style.width = progress + "%";
      currentSlideEl.textContent = currentIndex;
    }

    swiper.on("slideChange", updateProgress);
    updateProgress();

    clearInterval(waitForSwiper);
  }, 300);
});
</script>
